	text = {
		trigger = {
			1024 = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_turkish_minority }
				has_variable = TUR_turkish_population_stability_factor
				NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_turkish_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
			}
		}
		localization_key = TUR_turkish_population_1024_stability_factor_yes
	}
}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_variable = TUR_archipelago_vc_effect
			check_variable = { TUR_archipelago_vc_effect < 100 }
		}
		localization_key = ottoman_archipelago_vilayet_centralization_value_yes
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ottoman_archipelago_vilayet_separatist_sentiments
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				790 = {
					TUR_state_has_minority = yes
					TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes
					OR = {
						TUR_state_has_minority_stability_factor = yes
						TUR_state_has_minority_war_support_factor = yes
					}
				}
				975 = {
					TUR_state_has_minority = yes
					TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes
					OR = {
						TUR_state_has_minority_stability_factor = yes
						TUR_state_has_minority_war_support_factor = yes
					}
				}

					TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes
					OR = {
						TUR_state_has_minority_stability_factor = yes
						TUR_state_has_minority_war_support_factor = yes
					}
				}
				900 = {
					TUR_state_has_minority = yes
					TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes
					OR = {
						TUR_state_has_minority_stability_factor = yes
						TUR_state_has_minority_war_support_factor = yes
					}
				}
				164 = {
					TUR_state_has_minority = yes
					TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes
					OR = {
						TUR_state_has_minority_stability_factor = yes
						TUR_state_has_minority_war_support_factor = yes
					}
				}
				899 = {
					TUR_state_has_minority = yes
					TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes
					OR = {
						TUR_state_has_minority_stability_factor = yes

defined_text = {
	name = TUR_cyprus_vilayet_desc
	text = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_description_selected }
		localization_key = TUR_cyprus_vilayet_desc_yes
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_millet_system_description_selected } }
		localization_key = TUR_cyprus_vilayet_desc_no
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = ottoman_cyprus_vilayet_centralization
	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_state = {
				has_state_flag = TUR_cyprus
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_vilayet_centralization }
			}
		}
		localization_key = ottoman_cyprus_vilayet_centralization_yes
	}
}
